## §A Canonical diff summary

Production code: ~277 LOC

- `src/polaris_v6/queue/run_store.py` MOD — added `list_completed_runs_by_query_slug()` using existing `idx_runs_query_slug` index, finished_at ASC, defensive against missing-table/legacy-schema.
- `src/polaris_v6/api/app.py` MOD — register `pins_router` after `bundle_router`.
- `web/lib/api.ts` MOD — added `PinSnapshot` interface + `fetchPinList()` + `fetchPin()` using existing `authFetch` + `BACKEND_URL = "/api/v6"` (iter-1 P1 fix: in-house transport/auth).
- `web/lib/pin_replay_client.ts` NEW — thin re-export shim for ergonomic consumer imports.
- `web/lib/pin_replay_demo.ts` — DEMO_PIN_REGISTRY data DELETED (47 lines), kept as empty object + type re-export shim.
- `web/app/pin_replay/page.tsx` MOD — empty-state guard added BEFORE detectRegressions/delta math (iter-1 P2 fix); existing snapshot-card rendering preserved for when registry is non-empty.

Tests + Playwright: ~397 LOC
- `tests/v6/test_pins_route.py` NEW — 9 tests covering: success path synthesis, abort_no_verified_sections shape variant, multi-run chronological ordering, unknown run 404, in-progress/aborted-corpus exclusion, exact date match, date mismatch 404, malformed date 422, zero-denominator pass_rate.
- `web/tests/e2e/{pin_replay,pin_replay_diff,pin_regression_alert,pin_retraction_handled}.spec.ts` — wrapped in `test.describe.skip(...)` with Seq 29 / #619 pointer (iter-1 P1 fix + iter-2 P2 confirmation).
- `web/tests/e2e/visual_60_baselines.spec.ts` — F13 row commented out (iter-1 P1 fix).
- `web/tests/e2e/perf_core_web_vitals.spec.ts` — `test.skip()` the INP-on-pin_replay click test (iter-2 P2.1 fix).

## §C Codex Red-Team checklist

1. Synthesis math correctness — abort variant returns pass_rate=0 even when generator has no sentences_dropped key (test_pass_rate_zero_denominator_returns_zero).
2. Auth contract — fetchPinList/fetchPin use `authFetch` (private) via `api.ts` exports; 401 routes to /sign-in.
3. Date validation — `len(date) != 10` + `date[4] != "-"` + `date[7] != "-"` → 422 (test_get_pin_by_date_malformed_returns_422).
4. Duplicate date disambiguation — get_pin_by_date matches BOTH run_id AND finished_at[:10] (not ambiguous).
5. Excluded statuses — `abort_corpus_inadequate` + `abort_scope_rejected` excluded; `partial_*` included (test_list_pins_excludes_in_progress_and_aborted_corpus).
6. Missing manifest.json on disk — `_load_manifest()` returns None, excludes that run from list (no 500).
7. Path traversal — `{run_id}` and `{date}` come through FastAPI path params; no direct file path construction from user input beyond `Path(artifact_dir) / "manifest.json"` where artifact_dir comes from run_store, not user.
8. Empty list semantics — list endpoint returns `[]` only if no qualifying siblings; unknown run_id is 404.
9. The frontend page.tsx empty-state guard runs at FIRST conditional after useState; subsequent code paths require non-empty PIN_DATES.
10. CI workflow does NOT need new env vars; `PYTHONPATH=src` already set for tests/v6/ job per `.github/workflows/web_ci.yml`.

+"""Pin replay route — I-cd-017 (#627).
+
+GET /runs/{run_id}/pins → list of PinSnapshot synthesized from all
+completed runs sharing the same query_slug (chronological by finished_at).
+
+GET /runs/{run_id}/pins/{date} → single PinSnapshot for the exact
+(run_id, finished_at[:10]) pair.
+
+Synthesis sources (iter-2 P1 fixes):
+- Pipeline status: `RunStatusResponse.pipeline_status` from run_store
+  (NOT raw manifest field — actors.py:219 translates `manifest.status` →
+  `pipeline_status`).
+- Quality fields: `manifest.json` `generator` block. Handles BOTH shape
+  variants:
+    * success path → `sections_kept`, `sentences_dropped`,
+      `outline_sections`, `sentences_verified`.
+    * abort_no_verified_sections path → `sections_total`,
+      `sections_dropped`, `sentences_verified` (NO `sections_kept`, NO
+      `sentences_dropped` — confirmed at
+      scripts/run_honest_sweep_r3.py:2468-2473).
+
+Auth: protected via app-level `dependencies=[Depends(_require_auth)]`.
+"""
+
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+import json
+from pathlib import Path
+from typing import Final
+
+from fastapi import APIRouter, HTTPException
+
+from polaris_v6.queue import run_store
+from polaris_v6.schemas.pin_snapshot import PinSnapshot
+from polaris_v6.schemas.run_status import RunStatusResponse
+
+router = APIRouter(prefix="/runs", tags=["pins"])
+
+_QUALIFYING_STATUSES: Final[frozenset[str]] = frozenset(
+    {
+        "success",
+        "partial_outline_fallback",
+        "partial_evaluator_advisory",
+        "partial_thin_corpus",
+        "partial_incomplete_corpus",
+        "partial_rule_check_warnings",
+        "abort_no_verified_sections",
+    }
+)
+
+
+def _collapsed_verdict(pipeline_status: str) -> str:
+    if pipeline_status == "abort_no_verified_sections":
+        return "abort_no_verified_sections"

## §C Codex Red-Team checklist

1. Synthesis math correctness — abort variant returns pass_rate=0 even when generator has no sentences_dropped key (test_pass_rate_zero_denominator_returns_zero).
2. Auth contract — fetchPinList/fetchPin use `authFetch` (private) via `api.ts` exports; 401 routes to /sign-in.
3. Date validation — `len(date) != 10` + `date[4] != "-"` + `date[7] != "-"` → 422 (test_get_pin_by_date_malformed_returns_422).
4. Duplicate date disambiguation — get_pin_by_date matches BOTH run_id AND finished_at[:10] (not ambiguous).
5. Excluded statuses — `abort_corpus_inadequate` + `abort_scope_rejected` excluded; `partial_*` included (test_list_pins_excludes_in_progress_and_aborted_corpus).
6. Missing manifest.json on disk — `_load_manifest()` returns None, excludes that run from list (no 500).
7. Path traversal — `{run_id}` and `{date}` come through FastAPI path params; no direct file path construction from user input beyond `Path(artifact_dir) / "manifest.json"` where artifact_dir comes from run_store, not user.
8. Empty list semantics — list endpoint returns `[]` only if no qualifying siblings; unknown run_id is 404.
9. The frontend page.tsx empty-state guard runs at FIRST conditional after useState; subsequent code paths require non-empty PIN_DATES.
10. CI workflow does NOT need new env vars; `PYTHONPATH=src` already set for tests/v6/ job per `.github/workflows/web_ci.yml`.

   2:

   5:

   8:

  12:   `pipeline_status`).
  13: - Quality fields: `manifest.json` `generator` block. Handles BOTH shape
  14:   variants:
  15:     * success path → `sections_kept`, `sentences_dropped`,
  16:       `outline_sections`, `sentences_verified`.
  17:     * abort_no_verified_sections path → `sections_total`,
  18:       `sections_dropped`, `sentences_verified` (NO `sections_kept`, NO
  19:       `sentences_dropped` — confirmed at
  20:       scripts/run_honest_sweep_r3.py:2468-2473).

  22: Auth: protected via app-level `dependencies=[Depends(_require_auth)]`.
  23: """

  26: 
  27: import json
  28: from pathlib import Path
  29: from typing import Final
  30: 
  31: from fastapi import APIRouter, HTTPException
  32: 
  33: from polaris_v6.queue import run_store
  34: from polaris_v6.schemas.pin_snapshot import PinSnapshot
  35: from polaris_v6.schemas.run_status import RunStatusResponse
  36: 
  37: router = APIRouter(prefix="/runs", tags=["pins"])
  38: 
  39: _QUALIFYING_STATUSES: Final[frozenset[str]] = frozenset(
  40:     {
  41:         "success",
  42:         "partial_outline_fallback",
  43:         "partial_evaluator_advisory",
  44:         "partial_thin_corpus",
  45:         "partial_incomplete_corpus",
  46:         "partial_rule_check_warnings",
  47:         "abort_no_verified_sections",
  48:     }
  49: )
  50: 
  51: 
  52: def _collapsed_verdict(pipeline_status: str) -> str:
  53:     if pipeline_status == "abort_no_verified_sections":
  54:         return "abort_no_verified_sections"
  55:     return "success"
  56: 
  57: 
  58: def _synthesize_pin_from_manifest(
  59:     run: RunStatusResponse,
  60:     manifest: dict,
  61: ) -> PinSnapshot:
  62:     """Build a PinSnapshot from a completed-run RunStatusResponse + manifest.
  63: 
  64:     Defensive against the two generator-block shape variants (iter-2 P1.2):
  65:     success-path manifests carry `sections_kept` + `sentences_dropped`;
  66:     abort_no_verified_sections manifests carry `sections_total` +
  67:     `sections_dropped` and lack `sentences_dropped`.
  68:     """
  69:     generator = manifest.get("generator") or {}
  70:     sections_kept = generator.get("sections_kept")
  71:     sections_dropped_in_generator = generator.get("sections_dropped")
  72:     sections_total = generator.get("sections_total")
  73:     outline_len = len(generator.get("outline_sections") or [])
  74: 
  75:     if sections_kept is None and sections_total is not None:
  76:         sections_kept = max(0, sections_total - (sections_dropped_in_generator or 0))
  77:     if sections_kept is None:
  78:         sections_kept = 0
  79: 
  80:     if sections_dropped_in_generator is not None:
  81:         section_count_dropped = sections_dropped_in_generator
  82:     elif outline_len > 0:
  83:         section_count_dropped = max(0, outline_len - sections_kept)
  84:     else:
  85:         section_count_dropped = 0
  86: 
  87:     verified = max(0, int(generator.get("sentences_verified") or 0))
  88:     dropped_sentences = max(0, int(generator.get("sentences_dropped") or 0))
  89:     denominator = verified + dropped_sentences
  90:     pass_rate = verified / denominator if denominator > 0 else 0.0
  91:     pass_rate = min(1.0, max(0.0, pass_rate))
  92: 
  93:     finished_at = run.finished_at or ""
  94:     pin_date = finished_at[:10] if finished_at else "1970-01-01"
  95: 
  96:     return PinSnapshot(
  97:         run_id=run.run_id,
  98:         pin_date=pin_date,
  99:         query=run.question,
 100:         verdict=_collapsed_verdict(run.pipeline_status or "error_unexpected"),
 101:         section_count_kept=max(0, sections_kept),
 102:         section_count_dropped=max(0, section_count_dropped),
 103:         verified_sentence_count=verified,
 104:         pass_rate=pass_rate,
 105:         retracted_source_ids=None,
 106:     )
 107: 
 108: 
 109: def _load_manifest(artifact_dir: str | None) -> dict | None:
 110:     if not artifact_dir:
 111:         return None
 112:     path = Path(artifact_dir) / "manifest.json"
 113:     if not path.is_file():
 114:         return None
 115:     try:
 116:         return json.loads(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
 117:     except (OSError, json.JSONDecodeError):
 118:         return None
 119: 
 120: 
 121: def _qualifies(run: RunStatusResponse) -> bool:
 122:     if run.lifecycle_status != "completed":
 123:         return False
 124:     pipeline_status = run.pipeline_status or ""
 125:     return pipeline_status in _QUALIFYING_STATUSES
 126:

 128: @router.get("/{run_id}/pins", response_model=list[PinSnapshot])
 129: def list_pins(run_id: str) -> list[PinSnapshot]:
 130:     anchor = run_store.get_run(run_id)
 131:     if anchor is None:
 132:         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"Run {run_id!r} not found.")
 133:     query_slug = anchor.query_slug
 134:     if not query_slug:
 135:         raise HTTPException(
 136:             status_code=404,
 137:             detail=f"Run {run_id!r} has no query_slug (run not yet completed by pipeline).",
 138:         )
 139:     siblings = run_store.list_completed_runs_by_query_slug(query_slug)
 140:     snapshots: list[PinSnapshot] = []
 141:     for run in siblings:
 142:         if not _qualifies(run):
 143:             continue
 144:         manifest = _load_manifest(run.artifact_dir)
 145:         if manifest is None:
 146:             continue
 147:         snapshots.append(_synthesize_pin_from_manifest(run, manifest))
 148:     return snapshots
 149: 
 150: 
 151: @router.get("/{run_id}/pins/{date}", response_model=PinSnapshot)
 152: def get_pin_by_date(
 153:     run_id: str,
 154:     date: str,
 155: ) -> PinSnapshot:
 156:     if len(date) != 10 or date[4] != "-" or date[7] != "-":
 157:         raise HTTPException(status_code=422, detail="date must be YYYY-MM-DD")
 158:     run = run_store.get_run(run_id)
 159:     if run is None or not _qualifies(run):
 160:         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"Run {run_id!r} not pin-eligible.")
 161:     finished_at = run.finished_at or ""
 162:     if finished_at[:10] != date:
 163:         raise HTTPException(
 164:             status_code=404,
 165:             detail=f"Run {run_id!r} finished on {finished_at[:10]!r}, not {date!r}.",
 166:         )
 167:     manifest = _load_manifest(run.artifact_dir)
 168:     if manifest is None:
 169:         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"Manifest missing for run {run_id!r}.")
 170:     return _synthesize_pin_from_manifest(run, manifest)

  35:     )

 succeeded in 1063ms:
   1: """SQLite-backed run-status store for POLARIS v6 Dramatiq queue.
   2: 
   3: I-arch-001a (2026-05-12):
   4: - Migration: RENAME COLUMN status → lifecycle_status (SQLite 3.25+)
   5: - New columns: query_slug, manifest_run_id, artifact_dir, pipeline_status,
   6:   cost_usd, decision_id (all nullable; backward-compatible)
   7: - New helpers: mark_failed, mark_aborted, set_pipeline_meta
   8: - get_run returns the full RunStatusResponse with new optional fields
   9: 
  10: I-rdy-011 (2026-05-16): cancellation support.
  11: - New column: cancel_requested (INTEGER 0/1).
  12: - request_cancel: queued → cancelled atomically (T1, instant); in_progress
  13:   → set the cancel flag (T2, cooperative — the worker observes it).
  14: - mark_in_progress is now a compare-and-swap (only transitions a queued,
  15:   not-cancel-requested row) so a queued cancel cannot be overwritten.
  16: - is_cancel_requested / mark_cancelled support the worker's cooperative
  17:   abort path.
  18: 
  19: I-rdy-013 (2026-05-16): 1-concurrent-session enforcement.
  20: - get_active_run: read-side helper — the run currently holding the session.
  21: - insert_run_if_idle: atomic check-and-insert (BEGIN IMMEDIATE) used by
  22:   POST /runs so a 2nd concurrent request cannot start a parallel session.
  23: - init_db serialized by `_INIT_LOCK`; `_connect` sets `busy_timeout`.
  24: 
  25: Default DB path: state/v6_runs.sqlite (gitignored). Override via env
  26: `POLARIS_V6_RUN_DB`. WAL mode enabled.
  27: """
  28: 
  29: from __future__ import annotations
  30: 
  31: import json
  32: import os
  33: import sqlite3
  34: import threading
  35: from datetime import datetime, timezone
  36: from typing import Any
  37: 
  38: from polaris_v6.schemas.run_status import RunStatusResponse
  39: 
  40: DEFAULT_DB_PATH = "state/v6_runs.sqlite"
  41: ENV_DB_PATH = "POLARIS_V6_RUN_DB"
  42: 
  43: # Lifecycle states from which a run can no longer transition. Public so the
  44: # /runs/{id}/cancel endpoint shares one definition of "terminal".
  45: TERMINAL_STATUSES = ("completed", "failed", "cancelled")
  46: 
  47: # Columns selected by get_run (single source of truth for both the
  48: # first-attempt and post-migration-retry queries).
  49: _RUN_COLUMNS = (
  50:     "run_id, template, question, lifecycle_status, pipeline_status, "
  51:     "queued_at, started_at, finished_at, result_json, error_json, "
  52:     "query_slug, manifest_run_id, artifact_dir, cost_usd, decision_id, "
  53:     "cancel_requested"
  54: )
  55: 
  56: # I-rdy-013: lifecycle states that count as an active research session. A run
  57: # in one of these blocks a new POST /runs (1-concurrent-session constraint).
  58: # `completed`, `cancelled`, `failed` are terminal and free the session slot.
  59: _ACTIVE_STATUSES = ("queued", "in_progress")
  60: 
  61: # I-rdy-013: serializes init_db across in-process threads so two concurrent
  62: # first requests cannot collide inside `PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL` or the schema
  63: # migration and raise sqlite3.OperationalError before the atomic gate runs.
  64: _INIT_LOCK = threading.Lock()
  65: 
  66: 
  67: def _resolve_path(path: str | None) -> str:
  68:     if path is not None:
  69:         return path
  70:     return os.environ.get(ENV_DB_PATH, DEFAULT_DB_PATH)
  71: 
  72: 
  73: def _now_iso() -> str:
  74:     return datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()
  75: 
  76: 
  77: def _connect(path: str | None = None) -> sqlite3.Connection:
  78:     resolved = _resolve_path(path)
  79:     parent = os.path.dirname(resolved)
  80:     if parent:
  81:         os.makedirs(parent, exist_ok=True)
  82:     conn = sqlite3.connect(resolved)
  83:     conn.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
  84:     # I-rdy-013: a concurrent writer waits up to 5s for the write lock
  85:     # instead of raising SQLITE_BUSY immediately (the issue's "no crash").
  86:     conn.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=5000")
  87:     return conn
  88: 
  89: 
  90: def _migrate_schema(conn: sqlite3.Connection) -> None:
  91:     """Idempotent additive migration. Safe to call on every init_db.
  92: 
  93:     1. Create base table if absent.
  94:     2. If legacy `status` column exists and `lifecycle_status` doesn't,
  95:        RENAME COLUMN to preserve values (SQLite 3.25+, Python 3.11 ships
  96:        SQLite 3.34+).
  97:     3. ADD COLUMN for each I-arch-001a / I-rdy-011 field if missing.
  98:     4. CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS for query lookups.
  99:     """
 100:     conn.execute(
 101:         """

 103:             run_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
 104:             template TEXT NOT NULL,
 105:             question TEXT NOT NULL,
 106:             lifecycle_status TEXT NOT NULL,
 107:             queued_at TEXT NOT NULL,
 108:             started_at TEXT,
 109:             finished_at TEXT,
 110:             result_json TEXT,
 111:             error_json TEXT
 112:         )
 113:         """
 114:     )
 115:     cols = {row[1] for row in conn.execute("PRAGMA table_info(runs)").fetchall()}
 116:     if "status" in cols and "lifecycle_status" not in cols:
 117:         conn.execute("ALTER TABLE runs RENAME COLUMN status TO lifecycle_status")
 118:         cols.discard("status")
 119:         cols.add("lifecycle_status")
 120:     for col_name, col_type in {
 121:         "query_slug": "TEXT",
 122:         "manifest_run_id": "TEXT",
 123:         "artifact_dir": "TEXT",
 124:         "pipeline_status": "TEXT",
 125:         "cost_usd": "REAL",
 126:         "decision_id": "TEXT",

 128:     }.items():

 130:             conn.execute(f"ALTER TABLE runs ADD COLUMN {col_name} {col_type}")

 135: def init_db(path: str | None = None) -> None:
 136:     """Create the runs table if absent, run migrations. Idempotent.
 137: 
 138:     I-rdy-013: serialized by `_INIT_LOCK` so two concurrent first requests
 139:     (FastAPI worker threads, one process) cannot collide inside
 140:     `PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL` or the schema migration and raise
 141:     sqlite3.OperationalError before the atomic gate is reached.
 142:     """
 143:     with _INIT_LOCK:
 144:         conn = _connect(path)
 145:         try:
 146:             conn.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL")
 147:             _migrate_schema(conn)
 148:             conn.commit()
 149:         finally:
 150:             conn.close()

 153: def insert_run(run_id: str, template: str, question: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> None:
 154:     """Insert a new row with lifecycle_status='queued'. Raises IntegrityError on duplicate.
 155: 
 156:     Unconditional primitive — does NOT enforce the 1-concurrent-session
 157:     constraint. POST /runs uses `insert_run_if_idle`; this remains for test
 158:     fixtures and any caller that deliberately wants an unconditional insert.
 159:     """
 160:     init_db(path)
 161:     conn = _connect(path)
 162:     try:
 163:         conn.execute(
 164:             "INSERT INTO runs (run_id, template, question, lifecycle_status, queued_at) "
 165:             "VALUES (?, ?, ?, 'queued', ?)",
 166:             (run_id, template, question, _now_iso()),
 167:         )
 168:         conn.commit()
 169:     finally:
 170:         conn.close()
 171: 
 172: 
 173: def insert_run_if_idle(
 174:     run_id: str, template: str, question: str, *, path: str | None = None
 175: ) -> RunStatusResponse | None:
 176:     """Atomically insert a new queued run IFF no run is currently active.
 177: 
 178:     I-rdy-013 (1-concurrent-session enforcement): the check-for-active and
 179:     the INSERT run inside one `BEGIN IMMEDIATE` transaction, so two
 180:     concurrent POST /runs cannot both pass the check. `BEGIN IMMEDIATE`
 181:     takes the write lock up-front; the 2nd writer blocks on it (up to the
 182:     `busy_timeout`) until the 1st commits, then sees the inserted row.
 183: 
 184:     Returns None when the run was inserted; returns the blocking active
 185:     RunStatusResponse when rejected (caller raises HTTP 409).
 186:     """
 187:     init_db(path)
 188:     placeholders = ", ".join("?" for _ in _ACTIVE_STATUSES)
 189:     conn = _connect(path)
 190:     conn.isolation_level = None  # manual transaction control
 191:     try:
 192:         conn.execute("BEGIN IMMEDIATE")
 193:         row = conn.execute(
 194:             f"SELECT {_RUN_COLUMNS} FROM runs "
 195:             f"WHERE lifecycle_status IN ({placeholders}) "
 196:             "ORDER BY queued_at LIMIT 1",
 197:             _ACTIVE_STATUSES,
 198:         ).fetchone()
 199:         if row is not None:
 200:             conn.execute("ROLLBACK")
 201:             return _row_to_response(row)
 202:         conn.execute(
 203:             "INSERT INTO runs (run_id, template, question, lifecycle_status, queued_at) "
 204:             "VALUES (?, ?, ?, 'queued', ?)",
 205:             (run_id, template, question, _now_iso()),
 206:         )
 207:         conn.execute("COMMIT")
 208:         return None
 209:     finally:
 210:         conn.close()
 211: 
 212: 
 213: def mark_in_progress(run_id: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> bool:
 214:     """Transition queued → in_progress IFF the run is not cancel-requested.
 215: 
 216:     I-rdy-011: compare-and-swap. The `WHERE lifecycle_status='queued' AND
 217:     cancel_requested=0` guard means a queued cancel that already flipped the
 218:     row to 'cancelled' cannot be overwritten by a worker picking the run up.
 219: 
 220:     Returns True iff the row transitioned; False means the run was cancelled
 221:     (or already past 'queued') and the caller must not run the pipeline.
 222:     """
 223:     conn = _connect(path)
 224:     try:
 225:         cur = conn.execute(
 226:             "UPDATE runs SET lifecycle_status='in_progress', started_at=? "
 227:             "WHERE run_id=? AND lifecycle_status='queued' AND cancel_requested=0",
 228:             (_now_iso(), run_id),
 229:         )
 230:         conn.commit()
 231:         return cur.rowcount > 0
 232:     finally:
 233:         conn.close()
 234: 
 235: 
 236: def request_cancel(run_id: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> str | None:
 237:     """Request cancellation of a run (I-rdy-011).
 238: 
 239:     - queued run → atomically transitioned to terminal 'cancelled' (T1,
 240:       instant — the worker's mark_in_progress CAS will then no-op).
 241:     - in_progress run → cancel_requested flag set; lifecycle stays
 242:       'in_progress' until the worker observes the flag at a pipeline stage
 243:       boundary and calls mark_cancelled (T2, cooperative).
 244: 
 245:     Returns the resulting lifecycle_status ('cancelled' or 'in_progress'),
 246:     or None if the run does not exist or is already terminal.
 247:     """
 248:     conn = _connect(path)
 249:     try:
 250:         # T1: queued → cancelled, atomically.
 251:         cur = conn.execute(
 252:             "UPDATE runs SET lifecycle_status='cancelled', cancel_requested=1, "
 253:             "finished_at=? WHERE run_id=? AND lifecycle_status='queued'",
 254:             (_now_iso(), run_id),
 255:         )
 256:         if cur.rowcount > 0:
 257:             conn.commit()
 258:             return "cancelled"
 259:         # T2: in_progress → set the flag for the worker to observe.
 260:         cur = conn.execute(

  19: import { authHeader, redirectToSignIn } from "@/lib/auth";
  20: 
  21: const BACKEND_URL = "/api/v6";
  22: 
  23: /**
  24:  * I-rdy-004 (#500) — fetch wrapper for every v6 API call. Injects the
  25:  * `Authorization: Bearer <jwt>` header, preserves any caller-supplied
  26:  * headers, and does NOT force a content-type (so `FormData` uploads keep
  27:  * their auto-generated multipart boundary). On a 401 it clears the token
  28:  * and routes to /sign-in.
  29:  */
  30: async function authFetch(
  31:   url: string,
  32:   init: RequestInit = {},
  33: ): Promise<Response> {
  34:   const headers = new Headers(init.headers ?? {});
  35:   for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(authHeader())) {
  36:     headers.set(key, value);
  37:   }
  38:   const response = await globalThis.fetch(url, { ...init, headers });
  39:   if (response.status === 401) {
  40:     redirectToSignIn();
  41:   }
  42:   return response;
  43: }
  44: 
  45: /**
  46:  * I-rdy-004 — SSE URL for a run's event stream. Native `EventSource` cannot
  47:  * set request headers, so the JWT rides as the `access_token` query param;
  48:  * the backend `require_auth` accepts it for `/stream/*` paths only.
  49:  */
  50: export function streamUrl(runId: string): string {
  51:   const token = authHeader().Authorization?.replace(/^Bearer /, "");
  52:   const base = `${BACKEND_URL}/stream/${encodeURIComponent(runId)}`;
  53:   return token ? `${base}?access_token=${encodeURIComponent(token)}` : base;
  54: }

  96: export interface ApiError extends Error {
  97:   status: number;
  98:   body: unknown;
  99: }

 101: async function asJsonOrThrow<T>(response: Response): Promise<T> {
 102:   const body = await response.json().catch(() => null);
 103:   if (!response.ok) {
 104:     const error = new Error(
 105:       `POLARIS backend returned ${response.status}`,
 106:     ) as ApiError;
 107:     error.status = response.status;
 108:     error.body = body;
 109:     throw error;
 110:   }
 111:   return body as T;
 112: }

 114: /**
 115:  * Thrown by createRun when POST /runs is rejected by the 1-concurrent-session
 116:  * constraint (I-rdy-013): a research run is already queued or in progress.
 117:  */
 118: export class ConcurrentRunError extends Error {
 119:   readonly activeRunId: string;
 120:   readonly activeStatus: string;
 121:   constructor(message: string, activeRunId: string, activeStatus: string) {
 122:     super(message);
 123:     this.name = "ConcurrentRunError";
 124:     this.activeRunId = activeRunId;
 125:     this.activeStatus = activeStatus;
 126:   }
 127: }

 129: export async function createRun(
 130:   payload: RunRequest,
 131: ): Promise<RunStatusResponse> {
 132:   const response = await authFetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/runs`, {
 133:     method: "POST",
 134:     headers: { "content-type": "application/json" },
 135:     body: JSON.stringify(payload),
 136:   });
 137:   if (response.status === 409) {
 138:     // Read the body exactly once, then unwrap FastAPI's { detail: {...} }
 139:     // envelope. The 1-concurrent-session reject carries a structured detail;
 140:     // any other 409 falls through to a generic ApiError.
 141:     const body = (await response.json().catch(() => null)) as {
 142:       detail?: unknown;
 143:     } | null;
 144:     const detail = (body?.detail ?? body) as {
 145:       code?: string;
 146:       message?: string;
 147:       active_run_id?: string;
 148:       active_status?: string;
 149:     } | null;
 150:     if (detail && detail.code === "concurrent_run_active") {
 151:       throw new ConcurrentRunError(
 152:         detail.message ?? "A research run is already in progress.",
 153:         detail.active_run_id ?? "",
 154:         detail.active_status ?? "in_progress",
 155:       );
 156:     }
 157:     const error = new Error("POLARIS backend returned 409") as ApiError;
 158:     error.status = 409;
 159:     error.body = body;
 160:     throw error;
 161:   }
 162:   return asJsonOrThrow<RunStatusResponse>(response);
 163: }

  96: export default function PinReplayPage() {
  97:   // I-cd-017 (#627): DEMO_PIN_REGISTRY removed — page falls back to empty
  98:   // state until Seq 29 / I-A-12 / #619 wires the live route client. The
  99:   // guard runs BEFORE detectRegressions / delta math (Codex iter-2 P2.2)
 100:   // so undefined snapshot dereferences cannot crash the empty-state path.
 101:   const [date_a, set_date_a] = useState(PIN_DATES[0] ?? "");
 102:   const [date_b, set_date_b] = useState(
 103:     PIN_DATES.includes("2026-04-30") ? "2026-04-30" : (PIN_DATES[0] ?? ""),
 104:   );
 105:   const [diff_open, set_diff_open] = useState(false);
 106: 
 107:   if (PIN_DATES.length === 0) {
 108:     return <EmptyPinReplay />;
 109:   }
 110: 
 111:   const snap_a = DEMO_PIN_REGISTRY[date_a];
 112:   const snap_b = DEMO_PIN_REGISTRY[date_b];
 113:   const all_snapshots = Object.values(DEMO_PIN_REGISTRY);
 114:   const alerts = detectRegressions(snap_a, snap_b);
 115: 
 116:   const delta_pass_rate =
 117:     Math.round(snap_b.pass_rate * 100) - Math.round(snap_a.pass_rate * 100);
 118:   const delta_sentences =
 119:     snap_b.verified_sentence_count - snap_a.verified_sentence_count;
 120: 
 121:   return (
 122:     <main className="bg-background text-foreground min-h-screen">
 123:       <div className="mx-auto max-w-5xl px-6 py-8">
 124:         <h1 className="text-2xl font-semibold tracking-tight">
 125:           Pin replay — same query on different dates
 126:         </h1>
 127:         <p className="text-muted-foreground mt-2 text-sm">
 128:           Sample pin-replay (demo data); production fetch from{" "}
 129:           <code>
 130:             /runs/{"{run_id}"}/pins/{"{date}"}
 131:           </code>{" "}
 132:           per M-INT-0b post-Carney.
 133:         </p>
 134:         {alerts.length > 0 ? (
 135:           <div
 136:             data-testid="regression-alert"
 137:             role="alert"
 138:             className="mt-4 rounded border border-rose-500/40 bg-rose-500/5 p-3 text-sm text-rose-700 dark:text-rose-300"
 139:           >
 140:             <strong className="block">⚠ Regression detected</strong>
 141:             <ul className="mt-1 space-y-1 text-xs">
 142:               {alerts.map((alert) => (
 143:                 <li
 144:                   key={alert.metric}
 145:                   data-testid={`regression-alert-${alert.metric}`}
 146:                 >
 147:                   {alert.metric}: dropped {alert.drop}
 148:                   {alert.unit === "pct" ? " pct points" : " sentences"} ( A=
 149:                   {alert.a_value}
 150:                   {alert.unit === "pct" ? "%" : ""}, B=
 151:                   {alert.b_value}
 152:                   {alert.unit === "pct" ? "%" : ""}, threshold=
 153:                   {alert.threshold}
 154:                   {alert.unit === "pct" ? " pct" : ""})
 155:                   {alert.attributed_to_retraction &&
 156:                   alert.attributed_to_retraction.length > 0 ? (
 157:                     <span
 158:                       data-testid="regression-retraction-attribution"
 159:                       className="text-muted-foreground ml-1"
 160:                     >
 161:                       (attributed to retraction of:{" "}
 162:                       {alert.attributed_to_retraction.join(", ")})
 163:                     </span>
 164:                   ) : null}
 165:                 </li>
 166:               ))}
 167:             </ul>
 168:           </div>
 169:         ) : null}
 170:         <div className="mt-6 grid grid-cols-1 gap-4 md:grid-cols-2">
 171:           <SnapshotCard
 172:             testid="pin-snapshot-a"
 173:             label="Snapshot A"
 174:             selected_date={date_a}
 175:             on_change={set_date_a}
 176:             snapshot={snap_a}
 177:           />
 178:           <SnapshotCard
 179:             testid="pin-snapshot-b"
 180:             label="Snapshot B"
 181:             selected_date={date_b}
 182:             on_change={set_date_b}
 183:             snapshot={snap_b}
 184:           />
 185:         </div>
 186:         <div className="mt-6">
 187:           <PinTimeseries snapshots={all_snapshots} />

 189:         <button
 190:           type="button"
 191:           data-testid="pin-show-diff"
 192:           onClick={() => set_diff_open(true)}
 193:           className="border-border mt-4 rounded border px-4 py-2 text-sm hover:bg-blue-500/10"
 194:         >
 195:           Show snapshot diff
 196:         </button>

 428: def get_run(run_id: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> RunStatusResponse | None:
 429:     """Return the run record or None if missing.
 430: 
 431:     Defensive against `OperationalError: no such table` so callers in stub
 432:     mode (e.g. `tests/v6/test_actors.py` direct `.fn()` invocation without
 433:     init_db) get None back, matching the actor's row-missing-stub-noop
 434:     contract.
 435: 
 436:     I-arch-001a Codex iter-2 P2-002: if a known DB exists with the legacy
 437:     schema, the first read-only `get_run` call would 500 on column-missing.
 438:     The defensive catch below detects "no such column" and triggers a
 439:     one-time migration via init_db before retrying.
 440:     """
 441:     conn = _connect(path)
 442:     try:
 443:         try:
 444:             row = conn.execute(
 445:                 f"SELECT {_RUN_COLUMNS} FROM runs WHERE run_id=?",
 446:                 (run_id,),
 447:             ).fetchone()
 448:         except sqlite3.OperationalError as exc:
 449:             msg = str(exc).lower()
 450:             # Narrow per Codex iter-1 P2-001: only the missing-table stub
 451:             # path returns None; surface other operational errors (schema
 452:             # corruption, migration faults) so they aren't masked as
 453:             # missing-row.
 454:             if "no such table" in msg:
 455:                 return None
 456:             # Codex iter-2 P2-002: legacy schema → migrate then retry once.
 457:             if "no such column" in msg:
 458:                 conn.close()
 459:                 init_db(path)
 460:                 conn = _connect(path)
 461:                 row = conn.execute(
 462:                     f"SELECT {_RUN_COLUMNS} FROM runs WHERE run_id=?",
 463:                     (run_id,),
 464:                 ).fetchone()
 465:             else:
 466:                 raise
 467:     finally:
 468:         conn.close()
 469:     if row is None:
 470:         return None
 471:     return _row_to_response(row)
 472: 
 473: 
 474: def get_active_run(*, path: str | None = None) -> RunStatusResponse | None:
 475:     """Return the oldest run still queued or in_progress, else None.
 476: 
 477:     I-rdy-013: read-side helper for the 1-concurrent-session constraint —
 478:     the run currently holding the session slot. At most one run is active
 479:     once `insert_run_if_idle` gates all inserts; the `ORDER BY queued_at`
 480:     is defensive (oldest first) for any pre-gate legacy rows.
 481: 
 482:     Defensive against a missing/legacy table, mirroring `get_run`.
 483:     """
 484:     placeholders = ", ".join("?" for _ in _ACTIVE_STATUSES)
 485:     query = (
 486:         f"SELECT {_RUN_COLUMNS} FROM runs "
 487:         f"WHERE lifecycle_status IN ({placeholders}) "
 488:         "ORDER BY queued_at LIMIT 1"
 489:     )
 490:     conn = _connect(path)
 491:     try:
 492:         try:
 493:             row = conn.execute(query, _ACTIVE_STATUSES).fetchone()
 494:         except sqlite3.OperationalError as exc:
 495:             msg = str(exc).lower()
 496:             if "no such table" in msg:
 497:                 return None
 498:             if "no such column" in msg:
 499:                 conn.close()
 500:                 init_db(path)
 501:                 conn = _connect(path)
 502:                 row = conn.execute(query, _ACTIVE_STATUSES).fetchone()
 503:             else:
 504:                 raise
 505:     finally:
 506:         conn.close()

 510: def list_completed_runs_by_query_slug(
 511:     query_slug: str, *, path: str | None = None
 512: ) -> list[RunStatusResponse]:
 513:     """List completed runs sharing a query_slug ordered by finished_at ASC.
 514: 
 515:     I-cd-017 (#627): pin-replay timeseries source. Uses the existing
 516:     `idx_runs_query_slug` index. Returns `[]` (not None) when no rows
 517:     match — callers distinguish "anchor run exists but no completed
 518:     siblings" from "anchor run unknown" via get_run() before calling.
 519:

 521:     """

 523:         f"SELECT {_RUN_COLUMNS} FROM runs "

 525:         "ORDER BY finished_at ASC"

 527:     conn = _connect(path)

 531:         except sqlite3.OperationalError as exc:
 532:             msg = str(exc).lower()

 534:                 return []
 535:             if "no such column" in msg:
 536:                 conn.close()
 537:                 init_db(path)
 538:                 conn = _connect(path)
 539:                 rows = conn.execute(query, (query_slug,)).fetchall()
 540:             else:
 541:                 raise
 542:     finally:
 543:         conn.close()
 544:     return [_row_to_response(row) for row in rows]

   1: """Run-status response schema.
   2: 
   3: I-arch-001a (2026-05-12): split lifecycle (operational) from pipeline_status
   4: (pipeline-A manifest verdict). Old `status` retained as computed alias for
   5: tests/v6/ backcompat — populated from lifecycle_status.
   6: 
   7: I-rdy-011 (2026-05-16): `cancel_requested` surfaced so the UI can show a
   8: cancel as in-flight in <5s, before an in-progress run reaches the next
   9: pipeline stage boundary and transitions to terminal `cancelled`.
  10: """
  11: 
  12: from __future__ import annotations
  13: 
  14: from typing import Literal
  15: 
  16: from pydantic import BaseModel, Field, computed_field
  17: 
  18: LifecycleStatus = Literal[
  19:     "queued",
  20:     "in_progress",
  21:     "completed",
  22:     "cancelled",
  23:     "failed",
  24: ]
  25: 
  26: PipelineStatus = Literal[
  27:     "success",
  28:     "partial_outline_fallback",
  29:     "partial_qwen_advisory",  # legacy alias (I-modref-004 #530) — historical manifests
  30:     "partial_evaluator_advisory",
  31:     "partial_thin_corpus",
  32:     "partial_incomplete_corpus",
  33:     "partial_rule_check_warnings",
  34:     "abort_scope_rejected",
  35:     "abort_corpus_inadequate",
  36:     "abort_corpus_approval_denied",
  37:     "abort_no_verified_sections",
  38:     "abort_no_sources",
  39:     "abort_evaluator_critical",
  40:     "error_unexpected",
  41: ]
  42: 
  43: # Backcompat alias used by older code/tests (tests/v6/ asserts body['status']
  44: # and record.status). Computed from lifecycle_status by the model.
  45: RunStatus = LifecycleStatus
  46: 
  47: 
  48: class RunStatusResponse(BaseModel):
  49:     run_id: str = Field(..., description="Server-assigned UUID hex.")
  50:     lifecycle_status: LifecycleStatus = Field(
  51:         ...,
  52:         description="Operational lifecycle: queued → in_progress → completed|failed|cancelled.",
  53:     )
  54:     pipeline_status: PipelineStatus | None = Field(
  55:         default=None,
  56:         description="Pipeline-A manifest verdict. NULL until run reaches a terminal pipeline state.",
  57:     )
  58:     template: str
  59:     question: str
  60:     queued_at: str = Field(..., description="ISO8601 UTC.")
  61:     started_at: str | None = None
  62:     finished_at: str | None = None
  63:     result_json: str | None = None
  64:     error_json: str | None = None
  65:     # I-arch-001a new optional fields for UUID/slug/artifact_dir mapping.
  66:     query_slug: str | None = None
  67:     manifest_run_id: str | None = None
  68:     artifact_dir: str | None = None
  69:     cost_usd: float | None = None
  70:     decision_id: str | None = None
  71:     # I-rdy-011: True once a cancel has been requested. For a queued run the
  72:     # request is applied atomically (lifecycle_status flips to 'cancelled');
  73:     # for an in_progress run this stays True while lifecycle_status is still
  74:     # 'in_progress', until the worker observes it at a stage boundary.
  75:     cancel_requested: bool = Field(
  76:         default=False,
  77:         description="True iff cancellation has been requested for this run.",
  78:     )
  79: 
  80:     @computed_field  # serialized in JSON and readable as attr

 succeeded in 1003ms:
   1: """Runs router — POST /runs, GET /runs/{id}, POST /runs/{id}/cancel.
   2: 
   3: I-phase0-005 (Codex APPROVE iter 4): persist runs to SQLite via
   4: polaris_v6.queue.run_store and enqueue the Dramatiq actor on POST.
   5: Replaces the previous in-memory `_run_table` dict.
   6: 
   7: I-rdy-010 (#506): POST /runs resolves uploaded `document_ids` to content
   8: BEFORE inserting/enqueuing the run, so a missing or unparsed upload fails
   9: loud here rather than leaving a queued orphan run. The resolved content is
  10: embedded in the actor message because the Dramatiq worker is a separate
  11: process and cannot read the API process's in-memory upload table.
  12: 
  13: I-rdy-011 (#507): POST /runs/{id}/cancel — a queued run cancels instantly;
  14: an in-progress run records the cancel request (the worker observes it at
  15: the next pipeline stage boundary). Already-terminal runs are an idempotent
  16: no-op.
  17: 
  18: I-rdy-013 (#509): POST /runs enforces the 1-concurrent-session constraint
  19: via `run_store.insert_run_if_idle` — a 2nd concurrent request is cleanly
  20: rejected with HTTP 409 (never enqueued) and a structured detail the
  21: frontend renders as a link to the active run.
  22: """
  23: 
  24: from __future__ import annotations
  25: 
  26: import sqlite3
  27: import uuid
  28: 
  29: from fastapi import APIRouter, HTTPException
  30: 
  31: from polaris_v6.api.upload import chunk_text, get_upload_record
  32: from polaris_v6.queue import run_store
  33: from polaris_v6.queue.actors import enqueue_research_run
  34: from polaris_v6.schemas.run_request import RunRequest
  35: from polaris_v6.schemas.run_status import RunStatusResponse
  36: 
  37: router = APIRouter(prefix="/runs", tags=["runs"])
  38: 
  39: 
  40: def _resolve_uploaded_documents(document_ids: list[str]) -> list[dict]:
  41:     """Resolve uploaded document_ids → content for actor-message embedding.
  42: 
  43:     Returns one dict per id: `{document_id, classification, filename,
  44:     chunks}`. `chunks` is `chunk_text(record.content)` — the full document
  45:     re-chunked (and capped), NOT the 3-chunk `chunk_preview`.
  46: 
  47:     Fails loud (HTTP 400) per LAW II on:
  48:       * a document_id with no upload record;
  49:       * an upload that yields no extractable text (e.g. an unparsed
  50:         pdf/docx) — a silent zero-evidence run would mislead the operator.
  51:     """
  52:     resolved: list[dict] = []
  53:     for document_id in document_ids:
  54:         record = get_upload_record(document_id)
  55:         if record is None:
  56:             raise HTTPException(
  57:                 status_code=400,
  58:                 detail=f"uploaded document {document_id!r} not found",
  59:             )
  60:         chunks = chunk_text(record.content)
  61:         if not chunks:
  62:             raise HTTPException(
  63:                 status_code=400,
  64:                 detail=(
  65:                     f"uploaded document {document_id!r} ({record.filename}) "
  66:                     "has no extractable text — pdf/docx parsing is not yet "
  67:                     "available; upload a .md or .txt document to ground a run."
  68:                 ),
  69:             )
  70:         resolved.append(
  71:             {
  72:                 "document_id": document_id,
  73:                 "classification": record.classification,
  74:                 "filename": record.filename,
  75:                 "chunks": chunks,
  76:             }
  77:         )
  78:     return resolved
  79: 
  80: 
  81: @router.post("", response_model=RunStatusResponse, status_code=202)
  82: def create_run(payload: RunRequest) -> RunStatusResponse:
  83:     # I-rdy-010: resolve uploads BEFORE insert_run/enqueue so a bad
  84:     # document_id fails loud here instead of orphaning a queued run.
  85:     uploaded_documents = _resolve_uploaded_documents(payload.document_ids)
  86: 
  87:     run_id = uuid.uuid4().hex
  88:     try:
  89:         # I-rdy-013: atomic 1-concurrent-session gate. Returns the blocking
  90:         # active run when rejected, None when this run was inserted.
  91:         active = run_store.insert_run_if_idle(
  92:             run_id, payload.template, payload.question
  93:         )
  94:     except sqlite3.IntegrityError as exc:
  95:         # uuid4 collision is theoretically impossible but defensive
  96:         raise HTTPException(status_code=409, detail=f"run {run_id!r} already exists") from exc
  97:     except RuntimeError as exc:
  98:         # init_db permission-denied or similar
  99:         raise HTTPException(status_code=503, detail=str(exc)) from exc
 100: 
 101:     if active is not None:
 102:         # I-rdy-013: 1-concurrent-session constraint — a research run is
 103:         # already queued or in progress. Reject cleanly; the rejected run is
 104:         # never enqueued (insert_run_if_idle rolled back — no row to clean
 105:         # up). The structured `detail` lets the frontend render a specific
 106:         # UX with a link to the active run.
 107:         raise HTTPException(
 108:             status_code=409,
 109:             detail={
 110:                 "code": "concurrent_run_active",
 111:                 "active_run_id": active.run_id,
 112:                 "active_status": active.lifecycle_status,
 113:                 "message": (
 114:                     "POLARIS runs one research session at a time. "
 115:                     f"Run {active.run_id[:8]} is currently {active.lifecycle_status}. "
 116:                     "Wait for it to finish before starting a new run."
 117:                 ),
 118:             },
 119:         )
 120: 
 121:     # The actor message carries the resolved upload content (the worker is
 122:     # a separate process — it cannot read the API process's upload table).
 123:     actor_payload = payload.model_dump()
 124:     actor_payload["uploaded_documents"] = uploaded_documents
 125:     try:
 126:         enqueue_research_run.send(run_id, actor_payload)
 127:     except Exception as exc:
 128:         # I-rdy-013 (Codex diff P1-001): the queued row is already committed.
 129:         # If enqueue fails it would never run yet would permanently hold the
 130:         # single-session slot. Mark it failed (terminal → frees the slot),
 131:         # then surface 503.
 132:         run_store.mark_failed(run_id, f"enqueue failed: {exc}")
 133:         raise HTTPException(
 134:             status_code=503,
 135:             detail=f"failed to enqueue run {run_id!r}: {exc}",
 136:         ) from exc
 137: 
 138:     record = run_store.get_run(run_id)
 139:     if record is None:  # pragma: no cover — insert just succeeded
 140:         raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="run row vanished after insert")
 141:     return record
 142: 
 143: 
 144: @router.get("/{run_id}", response_model=RunStatusResponse)
 145: def get_run(run_id: str) -> RunStatusResponse:
 146:     record = run_store.get_run(run_id)
 147:     if record is None:
 148:         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"run {run_id!r} not found")
 149:     return record
 150: 
 151: 
 152: @router.post("/{run_id}/cancel", response_model=RunStatusResponse)
 153: def cancel_run(run_id: str) -> RunStatusResponse:
 154:     """Request cancellation of a run (I-rdy-011 / #507).
 155: 
 156:     - Unknown run → 404.
 157:     - Already terminal (completed / failed / cancelled) → idempotent no-op,
 158:       returns the current record (200).
 159:     - queued → cancelled instantly; in_progress → cancel requested, the
 160:       worker aborts cooperatively at the next pipeline stage boundary.
 161:     """
 162:     record = run_store.get_run(run_id)
 163:     if record is None:
 164:         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"run {run_id!r} not found")
 165:     if record.lifecycle_status in run_store.TERMINAL_STATUSES:
 166:         return record  # idempotent — nothing to cancel
 167: 
 168:     run_store.request_cancel(run_id)
 169: 
 170:     updated = run_store.get_run(run_id)
 171:     if updated is None:  # pragma: no cover — the row existed a line ago
 172:         raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="run row vanished after cancel")
 173:     return updated

  11:  */
  12: 
  13: import { expect, test, type TestInfo } from "@playwright/test";
  14: 
  15: function chromium_only(info: TestInfo): void {
  16:   test.skip(
  17:     info.project.name !== "chromium",
  18:     "I-p2c-004 CWV measurements rely on chromium-only PerformanceObserver entries",
  19:   );
  20: }
  21: 
  22: test("LCP on /intake under 2500ms", async ({ page }, info) => {
  23:   chromium_only(info);
  24:   await page.addInitScript(() => {
  25:     (window as unknown as { __lcp_entries__: unknown[] }).__lcp_entries__ = [];
  26:     new PerformanceObserver((list) => {
  27:       const arr = (window as unknown as { __lcp_entries__: unknown[] })
  28:         .__lcp_entries__;
  29:       for (const e of list.getEntries()) arr.push(e);
  30:     }).observe({ type: "largest-contentful-paint", buffered: true });
  31:   });
  32:   await page.goto("/intake", { waitUntil: "domcontentloaded" });
  33:   await page.waitForTimeout(1500);
  34:   const lcp = await page.evaluate(() => {
  35:     const arr = (window as unknown as { __lcp_entries__: PerformanceEntry[] })
  36:       .__lcp_entries__;
  37:     if (arr.length === 0) return null;
  38:     return arr[arr.length - 1].startTime;
  39:   });
  40:   expect(lcp).not.toBeNull();
  41:   expect(lcp).toBeLessThan(2500);
  42: });
  43:

  54:     timeout: 30_000,

  56:   const data_timings = await results.getAttribute("data-timings");

  61:   const avg = timings.reduce((s, t) => s + t, 0) / timings.length;

  63: });

+// I-cd-017 (#627): pin-replay snapshot consumed by /pin_replay timeseries.
+// Mirrors PinSnapshot schema in src/polaris_v6/schemas/pin_snapshot.py.
+export interface PinSnapshot {
+  run_id: string;
+  pin_date: string;
+  query: string;
+  verdict: "success" | "abort_no_verified_sections";
+  section_count_kept: number;
+  section_count_dropped: number;
+  verified_sentence_count: number;
+  pass_rate: number;
+  retracted_source_ids?: string[] | null;
+}
+
+export async function fetchPinList(runId: string): Promise<PinSnapshot[]> {
+  const response = await authFetch(
+    `${BACKEND_URL}/runs/${encodeURIComponent(runId)}/pins`,
+  );
+  return asJsonOrThrow<PinSnapshot[]>(response);
+}
+
+export async function fetchPin(
+  runId: string,
+  date: string,
+): Promise<PinSnapshot> {
+  const response = await authFetch(
+    `${BACKEND_URL}/runs/${encodeURIComponent(runId)}/pins/${encodeURIComponent(date)}`,
+  );
+  return asJsonOrThrow<PinSnapshot>(response);
+}

diff --git a/src/polaris_v6/api/pins.py b/src/polaris_v6/api/pins.py
new file mode 100644
index 00000000..c50d55fa
--- /dev/null
+++ b/src/polaris_v6/api/pins.py
@@ -0,0 +1,170 @@
+"""Pin replay route — I-cd-017 (#627).
+
+GET /runs/{run_id}/pins → list of PinSnapshot synthesized from all
+completed runs sharing the same query_slug (chronological by finished_at).
+
+GET /runs/{run_id}/pins/{date} → single PinSnapshot for the exact
+(run_id, finished_at[:10]) pair.
+
+Synthesis sources (iter-2 P1 fixes):
+- Pipeline status: `RunStatusResponse.pipeline_status` from run_store
+  (NOT raw manifest field — actors.py:219 translates `manifest.status` →
+  `pipeline_status`).
+- Quality fields: `manifest.json` `generator` block. Handles BOTH shape
+  variants:
+    * success path → `sections_kept`, `sentences_dropped`,
+      `outline_sections`, `sentences_verified`.
+    * abort_no_verified_sections path → `sections_total`,
+      `sections_dropped`, `sentences_verified` (NO `sections_kept`, NO
+      `sentences_dropped` — confirmed at
+      scripts/run_honest_sweep_r3.py:2468-2473).
+
+Auth: protected via app-level `dependencies=[Depends(_require_auth)]`.
+"""
+
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+import json
+from pathlib import Path
+from typing import Final
+
+from fastapi import APIRouter, HTTPException
+
+from polaris_v6.queue import run_store
+from polaris_v6.schemas.pin_snapshot import PinSnapshot
+from polaris_v6.schemas.run_status import RunStatusResponse
+
+router = APIRouter(prefix="/runs", tags=["pins"])
+
+_QUALIFYING_STATUSES: Final[frozenset[str]] = frozenset(
+    {
+        "success",
+        "partial_outline_fallback",
+        "partial_evaluator_advisory",
+        "partial_thin_corpus",
+        "partial_incomplete_corpus",
+        "partial_rule_check_warnings",
+        "abort_no_verified_sections",
+    }
+)
+
+
+def _collapsed_verdict(pipeline_status: str) -> str:
+    if pipeline_status == "abort_no_verified_sections":
+        return "abort_no_verified_sections"
+    return "success"
+
+
+def _synthesize_pin_from_manifest(
+    run: RunStatusResponse,
+    manifest: dict,
+) -> PinSnapshot:
+    """Build a PinSnapshot from a completed-run RunStatusResponse + manifest.
+
+    Defensive against the two generator-block shape variants (iter-2 P1.2):
+    success-path manifests carry `sections_kept` + `sentences_dropped`;
+    abort_no_verified_sections manifests carry `sections_total` +
+    `sections_dropped` and lack `sentences_dropped`.
+    """
+    generator = manifest.get("generator") or {}
+    sections_kept = generator.get("sections_kept")
+    sections_dropped_in_generator = generator.get("sections_dropped")
+    sections_total = generator.get("sections_total")
+    outline_len = len(generator.get("outline_sections") or [])
+
+    if sections_kept is None and sections_total is not None:
+        sections_kept = max(0, sections_total - (sections_dropped_in_generator or 0))
+    if sections_kept is None:
+        sections_kept = 0
+
+    if sections_dropped_in_generator is not None:
+        section_count_dropped = sections_dropped_in_generator
+    elif outline_len > 0:
+        section_count_dropped = max(0, outline_len - sections_kept)
+    else:
+        section_count_dropped = 0
+
+    verified = max(0, int(generator.get("sentences_verified") or 0))
+    dropped_sentences = max(0, int(generator.get("sentences_dropped") or 0))
+    denominator = verified + dropped_sentences
+    pass_rate = verified / denominator if denominator > 0 else 0.0
+    pass_rate = min(1.0, max(0.0, pass_rate))
+
+    finished_at = run.finished_at or ""
+    pin_date = finished_at[:10] if finished_at else "1970-01-01"
+
+    return PinSnapshot(
+        run_id=run.run_id,
+        pin_date=pin_date,
+        query=run.question,
+        verdict=_collapsed_verdict(run.pipeline_status or "error_unexpected"),
+        section_count_kept=max(0, sections_kept),
+        section_count_dropped=max(0, section_count_dropped),
+        verified_sentence_count=verified,
+        pass_rate=pass_rate,
+        retracted_source_ids=None,
+    )
+
+
+def _load_manifest(artifact_dir: str | None) -> dict | None:
+    if not artifact_dir:
+        return None
+    path = Path(artifact_dir) / "manifest.json"
+    if not path.is_file():
+        return None
+    try:
+        return json.loads(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
+    except (OSError, json.JSONDecodeError):
+        return None
+
+
+def _qualifies(run: RunStatusResponse) -> bool:
+    if run.lifecycle_status != "completed":
+        return False
+    pipeline_status = run.pipeline_status or ""
+    return pipeline_status in _QUALIFYING_STATUSES
+
+
+@router.get("/{run_id}/pins", response_model=list[PinSnapshot])
+def list_pins(run_id: str) -> list[PinSnapshot]:
+    anchor = run_store.get_run(run_id)
+    if anchor is None:
+        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"Run {run_id!r} not found.")
+    query_slug = anchor.query_slug
+    if not query_slug:
+        raise HTTPException(
+            status_code=404,
+            detail=f"Run {run_id!r} has no query_slug (run not yet completed by pipeline).",
+        )
+    siblings = run_store.list_completed_runs_by_query_slug(query_slug)
+    snapshots: list[PinSnapshot] = []
+    for run in siblings:
+        if not _qualifies(run):
+            continue
+        manifest = _load_manifest(run.artifact_dir)
+        if manifest is None:
+            continue
+        snapshots.append(_synthesize_pin_from_manifest(run, manifest))
+    return snapshots
+
+
+@router.get("/{run_id}/pins/{date}", response_model=PinSnapshot)
+def get_pin_by_date(
+    run_id: str,
+    date: str,
+) -> PinSnapshot:
+    if len(date) != 10 or date[4] != "-" or date[7] != "-":
+        raise HTTPException(status_code=422, detail="date must be YYYY-MM-DD")
+    run = run_store.get_run(run_id)
+    if run is None or not _qualifies(run):
+        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"Run {run_id!r} not pin-eligible.")
+    finished_at = run.finished_at or ""
+    if finished_at[:10] != date:
+        raise HTTPException(
+            status_code=404,
+            detail=f"Run {run_id!r} finished on {finished_at[:10]!r}, not {date!r}.",
+        )
+    manifest = _load_manifest(run.artifact_dir)
+    if manifest is None:
+        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"Manifest missing for run {run_id!r}.")
+    return _synthesize_pin_from_manifest(run, manifest)

index 4de9bc68..4c8c605d 100644
--- a/src/polaris_v6/queue/run_store.py
+++ b/src/polaris_v6/queue/run_store.py
@@ -505,3 +505,40 @@ def get_active_run(*, path: str | None = None) -> RunStatusResponse | None:
     finally:
         conn.close()
     return None if row is None else _row_to_response(row)
+
+
+def list_completed_runs_by_query_slug(
+    query_slug: str, *, path: str | None = None
+) -> list[RunStatusResponse]:
+    """List completed runs sharing a query_slug ordered by finished_at ASC.
+
+    I-cd-017 (#627): pin-replay timeseries source. Uses the existing
+    `idx_runs_query_slug` index. Returns `[]` (not None) when no rows
+    match — callers distinguish "anchor run exists but no completed
+    siblings" from "anchor run unknown" via get_run() before calling.
+
+    Defensive against missing-table / legacy-schema like get_run.
+    """
+    query = (
+        f"SELECT {_RUN_COLUMNS} FROM runs "
+        "WHERE query_slug=? AND lifecycle_status='completed' "
+        "ORDER BY finished_at ASC"
+    )
+    conn = _connect(path)
+    try:
+        try:
+            rows = conn.execute(query, (query_slug,)).fetchall()
+        except sqlite3.OperationalError as exc:
+            msg = str(exc).lower()
+            if "no such table" in msg:
+                return []
+            if "no such column" in msg:
+                conn.close()
+                init_db(path)
+                conn = _connect(path)
+                rows = conn.execute(query, (query_slug,)).fetchall()
+            else:
+                raise
+    finally:
+        conn.close()
+    return [_row_to_response(row) for row in rows]
diff --git a/src/polaris_v6/schemas/pin_snapshot.py b/src/polaris_v6/schemas/pin_snapshot.py
new file mode 100644
index 00000000..d07e653b

+"""Pin snapshot schema — I-cd-017 (#627).
+
+Per-run synthesized quality snapshot keyed by completed_at ISO date.
+Synthesized from `manifest.json` + run_store fields; NO separate
+pin-write path in the v6 actor (Option B accepted by Codex
+scope-consult 2026-05-20 — full B writes a new actor path; iter-2 P1
+clarified manifest top-level uses `status` not `pipeline_status`).
+
+`PinSnapshot` is the contract consumed by `web/lib/pin_replay_client.ts`.
+`extra="forbid"` mirrors the BundleManifest v1.0 schema-freeze discipline
+landed in I-cd-012.
+"""
+
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+from pydantic import BaseModel, ConfigDict, Field
+
+
+class PinSnapshot(BaseModel):
+    """Per-run quality snapshot for pin-replay timeseries."""
+
+    model_config = ConfigDict(extra="forbid", frozen=True)
+
+    run_id: str = Field(..., description="Source run_id (multiple runs may share pin_date).")
+    pin_date: str = Field(..., pattern=r"^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$", description="ISO date of run completion.")
+    query: str = Field(..., description="Research question.")
+    verdict: str = Field(..., description="success | abort_no_verified_sections (partial_* collapsed to success).")
+    section_count_kept: int = Field(..., ge=0)
+    section_count_dropped: int = Field(..., ge=0)
+    verified_sentence_count: int = Field(..., ge=0)
+    pass_rate: float = Field(..., ge=0.0, le=1.0)
+    retracted_source_ids: list[str] | None = Field(
+        default=None,
+        description="Not captured today — placeholder for future source-retraction logging.",
+    )

import json, os, sqlite3, tempfile
from pathlib import Path
from fastapi.testclient import TestClient

os.environ['POLARIS_AUTH_DISABLED'] = '1'
from polaris_v6.queue import run_store
from polaris_v6.api.app import create_app

with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as td:
    db = Path(td) / 'runs.sqlite'
    os.environ[run_store.ENV_DB_PATH] = str(db)
    run_store.init_db(str(db))
    artifact = Path(td) / 'run'
    artifact.mkdir()
    (artifact / 'manifest.json').write_text(json.dumps({
        'status': 'partial_qwen_advisory',
        'generator': {
            'outline_sections': ['a','b'],
            'sections_kept': 2,
            'sentences_verified': 5,
            'sentences_dropped': 1,
        },
    }), encoding='utf-8')
    conn = sqlite3.connect(str(db))
    conn.execute(\"INSERT INTO runs (run_id, template, question, lifecycle_status, queued_at, started_at, finished_at, query_slug, artifact_dir, pipeline_status, cancel_requested) VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,0)\", ('r_qwen', 'clinical', 'Q', 'completed', '2026-01-01T00:00:00Z', '2026-01-01T00:00:00Z', '2026-05-20T00:00:00Z', 'q', str(artifact), 'partial_qwen_advisory'))
    conn.commit(); conn.close()
    client = TestClient(create_app())
    print('list', client.get('/runs/r_qwen/pins').status_code, client.get('/runs/r_qwen/pins').json())
    print('single', client.get('/runs/r_qwen/pins/2026-05-20').status_code, client.get('/runs/r_qwen/pins/2026-05-20').json())

from pathlib import Path

os.environ['POLARIS_AUTH_DISABLED'] = '1'
os.environ.pop('POLARIS_GPG_KEY_ID', None)
from fastapi.testclient import TestClient
from polaris_v6.queue import run_store
from polaris_v6.api.app import create_app

with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory(dir='C:/tmp') as td:
    db = Path(td) / 'runs.sqlite'
    os.environ[run_store.ENV_DB_PATH] = str(db)
    run_store.init_db(str(db))

    artifact.mkdir()

   1: /**
   2:  * I-f13-003: Inline regression alerts on the pin-replay page. Hard-coded
   3:  * thresholds; production reads from a regression-config file (post-Carney).
   4:  *
   5:  * I-f13-004: source-retraction context attribution for sentence-count drops.
   6:  */
   7: 
   8: import type { PinSnapshot } from "@/lib/pin_replay_demo";
   9: 
  10: export const REGRESSION_THRESHOLDS = {
  11:   pass_rate_pct_drop: 5,
  12:   verified_sentence_count_drop: 3,
  13: } as const;
  14: 
  15: export interface RegressionAlert {
  16:   metric: "pass_rate" | "verified_sentence_count";
  17:   a_value: number;
  18:   b_value: number;
  19:   drop: number;
  20:   threshold: number;
  21:   unit: "pct" | "count";
  22:   attributed_to_retraction?: string[];
  23: }
  24: 
  25: export interface RetractionContext {
  26:   newly_retracted: string[];
  27: }
  28: 
  29: export function getRetractionContext(
  30:   a: PinSnapshot,
  31:   b: PinSnapshot,
  32: ): RetractionContext {
  33:   const a_ids = a.retracted_source_ids ?? [];
  34:   const newly_retracted = (b.retracted_source_ids ?? []).filter(
  35:     (id) => !a_ids.includes(id),
  36:   );
  37:   return { newly_retracted };
  38: }
  39: 
  40: export function detectRegressions(
  41:   a: PinSnapshot,
  42:   b: PinSnapshot,
  43: ): RegressionAlert[] {
  44:   const alerts: RegressionAlert[] = [];
  45:   const retraction = getRetractionContext(a, b);
  46: 
  47:   const a_pass_pct = Math.round(a.pass_rate * 100);
  48:   const b_pass_pct = Math.round(b.pass_rate * 100);
  49:   const pass_drop = a_pass_pct - b_pass_pct;
  50:   if (pass_drop > REGRESSION_THRESHOLDS.pass_rate_pct_drop) {
  51:     alerts.push({
  52:       metric: "pass_rate",
  53:       a_value: a_pass_pct,
  54:       b_value: b_pass_pct,
  55:       drop: pass_drop,
  56:       threshold: REGRESSION_THRESHOLDS.pass_rate_pct_drop,
  57:       unit: "pct",
  58:     });
  59:   }
  60: 
  61:   const sentence_drop = a.verified_sentence_count - b.verified_sentence_count;
  62:   if (sentence_drop > REGRESSION_THRESHOLDS.verified_sentence_count_drop) {
  63:     const alert: RegressionAlert = {
  64:       metric: "verified_sentence_count",
  65:       a_value: a.verified_sentence_count,
  66:       b_value: b.verified_sentence_count,
  67:       drop: sentence_drop,
  68:       threshold: REGRESSION_THRESHOLDS.verified_sentence_count_drop,
  69:       unit: "count",
  70:     };
  71:     if (retraction.newly_retracted.length > 0) {
  72:       alert.attributed_to_retraction = retraction.newly_retracted;
  73:     }
  74:     alerts.push(alert);
  75:   }
  76: 
  77:   return alerts;
  78: }

  26: 
  27: function formatValue(value: unknown, kind: FieldKind, key: string): string {
  28:   if (kind === "numeric" && typeof value === "number") {
  29:     if (key === "pass_rate") return `${Math.round(value * 100)}%`;
  30:     return String(value);
  31:   }
  32:   return String(value ?? "");
  33: }
  34: 
  35: function computeDelta(
  36:   a: unknown,
  37:   b: unknown,
  38:   kind: FieldKind,
  39:   key: string,
  40: ): string {
  41:   if (kind === "numeric" && typeof a === "number" && typeof b === "number") {
  42:     const delta =
  43:       key === "pass_rate" ? Math.round(b * 100) - Math.round(a * 100) : b - a;
  44:     const prefix = delta > 0 ? "+" : "";
  45:     return key === "pass_rate" ? `${prefix}${delta}%` : `${prefix}${delta}`;
  46:   }
  47:   // String/categorical: report changed/unchanged.
  48:   return a === b ? "(unchanged)" : "(changed)";
  49: }
